Note: Xpanse is priced per Asset Under Management (AUM). AUM are calculated as the sum of 
(1) number of distinct IP addresses, (2) number of distinct SSL signing certificates, (3) number of
distinct fully qualified domain names, (4) number of distinct open services directly attributable to
customers, and (5) number of distinct cloud resources.   Quotes are also rounded up to the
nearest hundred AUM.
